Although it is an old hotel that has not been renovated for a while, it can be seen that it is well maintained.

Because we were in a hurry to catch the train at the train station, it was very time-consuming and affected our mood. Contacting the hotel customer service explained that if there is no renewal after 12 o'clock, the room card will be invalid, but what about the three hours between this and the check-out time at 3 o'clock? This is unreasonable.
Mr. Liu at the front desk and Ms. Xu at the customer service were professional and had a great attitude. They solved my problem. Thank you!
